  package_gnu='GNU '; \
else \
  package_gnu=''; \
fi; \

  msgid_bugs_address='http://bugzilla.gnome.org/'; \
else \
  msgid_bugs_address='http://bugzilla.gnome.org/enter_bug.cgi?product=GStreamer'; \
fi; \
case `/usr/bin/xgettext --version | sed 1q | sed -e 's,^[^0-9]*,,'` in \
  '' | 0.[0-9] | 0.[0-9].* | 0.1[0-5] | 0.1[0-5].* | 0.16 | 0.16.[0-1]*) \
    /usr/bin/xgettext --default-domain=gst-plugins-bad-0.10 --directory=.. \
      --add-comments=TRANSLATORS: --keyword=_ --keyword=N_  \
      --files-from=./POTFILES.in \
      --copyright-holder='' \
      --msgid-bugs-address="$msgid_bugs_address" \
    ;; \
  *) \
    /usr/bin/xgettext --default-domain=gst-plugins-bad-0.10 --directory=.. \
      --add-comments=TRANSLATORS: --keyword=_ --keyword=N_  \
      --files-from=./POTFILES.in \
      --copyright-holder='' \
      --package-name="${package_gnu}gst-plugins-bad" \
      --package-version='0.10.23' \
      --msgid-bugs-address="$msgid_bugs_address" \
    ;; \
esac

  if test -f ./gst-plugins-bad-0.10.pot; then \
    sed -f remove-potcdate.sed < ./gst-plugins-bad-0.10.pot > gst-plugins-bad-0.10.1po && \
    sed -f remove-potcdate.sed < gst-plugins-bad-0.10.po > gst-plugins-bad-0.10.2po && \
    if cmp gst-plugins-bad-0.10.1po gst-plugins-bad-0.10.2po >/dev/null 2>&1; then \
      rm -f gst-plugins-bad-0.10.1po gst-plugins-bad-0.10.2po gst-plugins-bad-0.10.po; \

      mv gst-plugins-bad-0.10.po ./gst-plugins-bad-0.10.pot; \
    fi; \
  else \
    mv gst-plugins-bad-0.10.po ./gst-plugins-bad-0.10.pot; \
  fi; \
}
